      <div class="alumni-stories">
       <div class="alumni-stories__header grid">
        <h2 class="alumni-stories__heading heading heading--one">
         Where will the RCA take you?
        </h2>
       </div>
       <div class="alumni-stories__carousel grid">
        <div class="carousel glide carousel" data-carousel="" data-slidetotal="3">
         <div class="carousel__container glide__track" data-glide-el="track">
          <ul aria-live="polite" class="carousel__slides glide__slides">
           <li class="carousel__item glide__slide">
            <div class="card card--image">
             <div class="card__container">
              <a aria-label="Curating as caring: ZoÃ© Whitley, Alumni Story" class="card__image-container" href="https://www.rca.ac.uk/news-and-events/rca-stories/curating-caring-zo%C3%A9-whitley-alumni-story/">
               <img alt="" src="https://rca-media.rca.ac.uk/images/DR_ZOE_WHITLEY_Curator_British_Pav.2e16d0ba.fill-878x472.jpg"/>
              </a>
              <div class="card__content-container">
               <div class="card__content">
                <div class="card__meta">
                 Alumni story
                </div>
                <h3 class="card__heading">
                 <a class="card__heading-link" href="https://www.rca.ac.uk/news-and-events/rca-stories/curating-caring-zo%C3%A9-whitley-alumni-story/">
                  Curating as caring: ZoÃ© Whitley, Alumni Story
                 </a>
                </h3>
                <div class="card__description">
                 <div class="rich-text">
                  ZoÃ© Whitley is Director of theÂ Chisenhale Gallery, London, having previously worked as a curator for the V&amp;A, Tate and Hayward Gallery. She curated the British Pavilion at the Venice Biennale in 2019, is one of the judges for the Turner Prize 2021 and is a member of the recently appointed Mayorâ€™s Commission for Diversity in the Public Realm. Whitley grew up in the USA, studying BA Art History in Swarthmore College, outside of Philadelphia, before coming to the UK in 2001 to study MA History of Design at the RCA and V&amp;A.
                 </div>
                </div>
               </div>
              </div>
             </div>
            </div>
           </li>
           <li class="carousel__item glide__slide">
            <div class="card card--image">
             <div class="card__container">
